* check-js-syntax: more exchanges
* linting enforced for 'y*.js' exchanges

* linting
* warn if exchange is skipped from test
* do not throw on 'Not Supported' (backwards compatible)
* don't retry on 'Not Supported' (non-recoverable) exception
* testOrderBook: stronger checks, added testL2OrderBook

## 1.6.1 (2017-09-04)

#### New Features

* (binance): correctly use ticker timestamp
#### Fixes

* use correct market type constant for OKX futures in watchOrders
* convert gtx time_in_force to po on binance
* add missing symbol assignment
* okex watchOrders() instrument type filter
* use symbol instead of market ID to map order books
* typo in exception name
* raise "Internal server error" as ExchangeNotAvailableError
* (binance): avoid requesting the extension of an undefined listen key
* fix variable declaration
